ExtraLinkedRef type 0x51 contract audit

xNVSE GameExtraData.h says ExtraLinkedRef is type 0x51 and size 0x10.
Crash register EDX dereferences to ExtraLinkedRef, while GetTypeID receives ECX=0xFFFFFDA5.
This script searches for type 0x51 users and compares them with type 0x52, the older ExtraLinkedRefChildren crash.
